the server is looking for a central
when the central is found and connected, the server notifies with batteryLevelChar.writeValue()

but if the central resets (I click the reset button) the server is stuck in ATT.cpp/HCIClass::sendAclPkt()
There is a buffer of 4 messages that fills up when the central resets.
